     var divs = document.querySelectorAll('.js-onboarding__loc-manager .primary .main-card .pre-link-div');      if (links && links.length && primaryLocation && primaryLocation.fullLocId) {        function forEach(collection, iteratee) {  var func = isArray(collection) ? arrayEach : baseEach;          break;        default:          url = ('https://api.weather.com/v2/turbo/vt1dailyforecast?apiKey=d522aa97197fd864d36b418f39ebb323&format=json&geocode='+eid+'&language='+locale+'&units=' + unit);
